 ) subhash chandra bose desh ke aise mahanayakon main se ek hai jinhone aazaadee kii ladaai ke liye apana sarvasv nyochaavar kar diya

 jaane subhash chandra bose kii 10 baaten
 
 
 1
 subhash chandra bose kaa janm 23 janvari, 1897 ko urisa ke katak shahar main hua tha
 His father's name was Jankinath Bose and mother's name was Prabhavati
 janakinath katak ke mashhoor vakil the
 2
 katak main praathmik shiksha puri karne ke baad unhone revensha koligiet skool main daakhila liya

 3
 unke pita kii ichha thi ki subhash isies bane
 He fulfilled this wish of his father
 1920 kii isies pariksha main unhone chauthaa sthaan paaya magar subhash kaa man angrejon ke adheen kaam karne kaa nahin tha

 4
 Subhash Chandra Bose first met Gandhiji on 20 July 1921
 gandhi ji kii salaah par ve bhartiya swatantraaa sangram ke liye kaam karne lage
 5
 ve jab kalakatta mahapalika ke pramukh adhikari bane to unhone kalakatta ke raaston kaa angreji naam hataakar bhartiya naam par kar diya
 6
 bharat kii aazaadee ke saath-saath unka judaav saamaajik kaaryon main bhi bana rahaa
 He had done the courageous task of transporting people surrounded by the fierce floods of Bengal to food, clothing and safe places
 samaaj seva kaa kaam niyamit rup se chalata rahe iske liye unhone 'yuvak-dal' kii sthapana kii
 7
 bhagat singh ko faansee kii sajaa se reeha karaane ke liye ve jail se prayaas kar rahe the

 is samjhaute ke tahat jail se bhartiya kaidiyon ke liye rihaai maangi gai thi

 is ghatana ke baad ve gandhi or congress ke kaam karne ke tareeke se bahut naaraaz ho gaye the
 8

 1934 i

 sunwaayee ke dauraan centre sarkaar ne court main ise sahi tehraate hue kaha tha ki supreme court is maamle main abhi sunwaayee kar saktaa kyonki iske liye notification jari nahin hua he

 What is Section 304 of the Indian Penal Code Generally Section 302 of the Indian Penal Code is imposed in murder cases
 lekin gaiyr iradatan hatya ke maamalon main dhara 302 nahin lagaai ja sakati
 There is a provision for imposing Section 304 of the Indian Penal Code in such cases
 abhinayta salmaan khan par isi dhara ke tahat maamla chal rahaa tha
 Section 304 is applicable in cases where the accused has no intention of killing anyone
 yaa aise maamle jinamein kisi kii maut to hoti he, par usamen kisi kaa iradatan dosha nahin hota

 1
 Food can be harmful by reheating the chickenchikan
 dobaaraa garm karne ke baad isamen maujuud protein compojishan badal jaataa he jisase pachan sambandhi samasyaayein ho sakati hai
 2
 aaluaalu swasthyavardhak hote hai lekin agar inhen banaakar bahut adhik der tak rakh diya jaae to inamen maujuud poshak tatv samaapt ho jate hai

 3
 Beetroot should never be reheated and eaten
 aisa karne se isamen maujuud nitrate samaapt ho jaataa he

 4
 Mushrooms should be tried that fresh mushrooms should always be eaten fresh

 5
 andyande ko dobaaraa garm karke khaanaa hameshaa nuksaandeh hota he
 The protein in the egg becomes toxic after reheating
 6
 Eating spinach again can also cause cancer
 isse cancer hone kaa khatra bad jaataa he
